< Review>
My son has attended Airborne's Mini Mach, Mach 1 and now their Mach 2 parkour classes. He also has celebrated 2 birthdays there. Those alone are worth 4 stars.

< Text>
I came here for a birthday party.

Parking is difficult!  It is in an office complex and I wasn't sure if I was parking in an approved spot or not.

The party was for 5 to 6 yr olds.  There was a separate sign in table for the birthday.  It would be helpful to know in advance that the children need to be barefoot, as some of the girls came wearing tights.  The staff was attentive to the kids.  There were bleachers on 1 side of the gym, where the parents could sit and watch.

After the play, the party continued upstairs.  There was additional bleacher  seating in front of a large window where you could see the entire gym floor below. There were also additional bathrooms upstairs.

The kids had a great time and the parents had an opportunity to talk.<//Text>

My son broke his arm so I called from the hospital as a courtesy to the gym let them know my daughter would not make it to her class.  While I had them on the phone I decided to schedule her make up class without my calendar in front of me. I later realized I would be out of town at the time I scheduled her make up so I called back the next day, the day BEFORE her make up was scheduled and they would not let me reschedule it. I had my own gymnastics program in AZ and this is the most ridiculous policy I've ever heard.  It's not like we missed our make up class and are trying to make up our make up!  I was essentially going to slide into a class in an hour that still had openings and open up room for the next day.  They kept telling me that they were saving a spot for me so IF someone called to do their make up then would have already told them no.  My thought was that it hasn't happened yet, so IF someone calls they could give it to them.  So sad they are willing to lose customer over not letting them attend a different make up ahead of time when there was room in both classes! I am withdrawing my daughter from the program.  When looking for a gym, we are essentially looking for a home.  We literally just paid and registration fee last week, attended one class and they won't refund our $50 registration fee either. They are clearly a money driven program and have terrible customer services.  The manager also told me there IS flexibility to this policy given the circumstance, but MY circumstance wasn't one of those.  When I asked to speak to the owner he told me she would just be referring me back to him since he was in charge of the recreation dept.</Text>

My husband took my 2013 ford edge to Central Auto Repair because the breaks were giving off a burnt odor as we were coming down the mountain from arrowhead.  This was March 7th 2019.  They had the car 2 days and said that problem was the front brake pads and calibers.  We paid $423.00 dollars and got them fixed.  However, after about 2 days of driving the vehicle I noticed the burnt smell had returned and the vehicle was becoming more increasing difficult to stop.  It began making a sound and the pedal was very mushy.    My husband returned the car to Central Auto Repair and they kept the vehicle until April 17th 2019 because they were having difficulty determining what the problem was.  When my husband picked up the vehicle this time, we were charged $792.00 because they said they had to replace the ABS unit, the break booster, break booster vacuum hose and the master cylinder. I struggled to get the vehicle to moved forward which caused the vehicle to violently jerk forward almost causing me to nearly ram the vehicle in front of me.  I had to have my vehicle towed from riverside to lake Elsinore ford.   The dealership found that the break caliber bolt was not properly tightened causing it to vibrate lose and fall out. <text>I've dined here many times because I live in the neighborhood. Today the udon was horrible, the outside mushy and falling apart while the inside was undercooked and chalky. The broth was palatable because it's probably a solid factory made concentrate. < review>
Selected a kitten to adopt, but had to wait over 30 days to take her home due to her being so young.  During that time, I visited her several times a week, when I noticed the kitten and her litter mates starting to get ill.  After alerting both the staff and management several times over the course of a few days, nothing was done, except to send the kitten off to be spayed.  After a vet had supposedly signed off on her health, I picked her up 2 days later noting she had thick nasal discharge and partially closed eyes.

After bringing her home, she fell critically ill, unable to eat or stand without falling over.  When she worsened after a misdiagnosis at  Aloha Animal Hospital in Vista, I took her to the Veterinary Specialty Hospital in Escondido.  Barely able to breath and clinging to life, there she was diagnosed with life-threatening bacterial, viral and parasite infections so severe and contagous, she was placed in isolation where she received IV fluids, meds and hand feeding with a dropper.  Although the cost for all this was several thousand dollars, this sweet little kitten pulled through.

To my chagrin, I contracted several of the infections and almost died, requiring emergency medical care.  Not only that, but also my 5 other cats also became ill and are having to undergo treatment.

I found out from an insider at this rescue that the kitten's litter mates and mother were all quaranteened the very next day after I picked up the kitten.  Yet, I did not receive even so much as a courtesy call from them alerting me to the possibility of a problem.  So not only are they willfully negligent in failing to heed my warning of the cage of cats becoming ill, but they are were also not responsible enough to call and warn me there could potentially be a problem with my kitten.  In addition, they are culpable in the expenses and heartache I and my animals have had to endure as a result of what should have been a simple and straight forward adoption.

As an animal behaviorist specializing in positive training to help animals with issues, I was going to volunteer my services at this rescue to help with some of the long-time unadopted cats.  But after this incident, I'm not willing to set foot back in this place for fear of what I might catch next.

So animal lover's beware - not only are you risking the health of your current pets should you adopt an animal from here, the life at stake could very well be your own...</review>

<Review>This place embodies why I moved to SLO over a decade ago.  Sure Miner's/ACE is a franchise but I challenge you to find another hardware store even another ACE where people are more interested in helping you.  If you don't go in there and get have someone there ask you if you need any help, you may want to check a mirror to see if you're invisible. Renovations done at this location were amazing. The place is looking great and the extra order lane in the drive-through is really nice. The location of this McDonalds is far from ideal though and something no amount of reservations can fix. It is crammed into a very busy corner of a shopping center and it can be difficult to get out of the drive-through after receiving your order as you have a stop sign and there's another stop sign for the traffic crossing directly in front of the exit from the drive-through and a that connects to a four way stop. The other thing this location has a problem with is consistency with the staff. I sat at the window while the man working the window laughed and had a conversation with two other female employee's while I waited and waited and WAITED for the single drink I had ordered even with trying to get their attention. Also, if you custom order something, for example with no onions or with extra pickles, chances are you are not going to get it the way you ordered it. So PLEASE be careful if you have food allergies.</Text>
